ControlType.Text | Конечно, Ана. Вот краткая выжимка способов выучить английский для ребёнка ~10 лет в Батуми — по форматам, от самого «носительского» к гибкому:
ControlType.Text |
ControlType.Text | 1. Языковые центры (группы) — основной офлайн-вариант.
ControlType.Text |  В Батуми их много, с детскими курсами. Проверенные адреса: Tamta's English Club (Горгасали 154, прямо для детей), British Centre (Лука Асатиани 58, метод Каллана), English Class (Чавчавадзе 54), Lingvo Lab (Лермонтова 18), English Rose (Грибоедова 63), S.T/The English Academy (Меликишвили 83). Лучший способ выбрать — открыть
ControlType.Text | 2gis.ge → Батуми → «школы иностранных языков»
ControlType.Text |  и звонить, уточняя детские летние группы.
ControlType.Text |
ControlType.Text | 2. Частный репетитор — самый гибкий и популярный путь.
ControlType.Text |  Индивидуально или мини-группой, под уровень ребёнка. Ищут через платформу
ControlType.Text | 5legko.com
ControlType.Text |  (раздел Батуми, ~1000–1200 ₽/час) или в Instagram (например, @evgeniya_englishteacher).
ControlType.Text |
ControlType.Text | 3. С носителем языка.
ControlType.Text |  В Батуми их меньше, чем в больших городах. Самый сильный «носительский» вариант на лето —
ControlType.Text | летняя школа GASB
ControlType.Text |  (Багратиони 117, преподаватели из США). Рядом, по тому же адресу,
ControlType.Text | American Corner
ControlType.Text |  при Посольстве США — там бывают бесплатные английские клубы и мероприятия (уточни детские активности).
ControlType.Text |
ControlType.Text | 4. Онлайн с носителем — то, что часто выбирают экспаты.
ControlType.Text |  Гибко и нередко дешевле живого носителя: Novakid (специально для детей), Preply, italki. Удобно совмещать с офлайн-кружком.
ControlType.Text |
ControlType.Text | 5. Среда и общение.
ControlType.Text |  Разговорные детские клубы при центрах, международные группы на кружках/спорте — английский «между делом».
ControlType.Text |
ControlType.Text | Если коротко под 10 лет:
ControlType.Text | репетитор или детская группа в центре для системности + летняя школа GASB или онлайн с носителем для живого языка.

"Super Minds is the latest edition of Cambridge University's English language course for children aged 5 to 12. The course takes children's English language skills to level A2 on the Common European Framework of Reference for Languages (CEFR).
ControlType.Text | The uniqueness of Super Minds lies in the fact that it is not just a language learning program, but is much more than just English.
ControlType.Text | The course includes teaching age-appropriate interdisciplinary topics such as mathematics, logic, science, history, literature, and more in English. At the same time, great attention is paid to the development of critical and creative thinking skills in children.
The Super Minds learning process, in addition to classical teaching, combines a variety of activities that are interesting for children, such as: theatrical performances, artistic writing, karaoke, video games, etc. Most importantly, all of this takes place in the target language, which immediately puts the learning material into an interesting and fun context for children.
ControlType.Text | Since Super Minds is a cutting-edge teaching method, the program is based on the use of modern digital technologies in the learning process, which further contributes to increasing the motivation to learn in 21st century children." - вставь это в документ

ControlType.Text | сделать каждый канал чек-боксом прямо внутри ячейки
ControlType.Text | : ставлю перед каждым каналом квадратик ⬜, а ты, когда отправила, меняешь его на ✅.

ControlType.Text |

ControlType.Text |

ControlType.Text |
ControlType.Text | ⬜ Instagram: @gasbatumi
ControlType.Text |
ControlType.Text | Как пользоваться:
ControlType.Text |  дважды кликни по ячейке, чтобы войти в режим редактирования, и замени ⬜ на ✅ напротив того канала, куда уже отправила. Так сразу видно: куда написала, а куда ещё нет. (Если ✅ неудобно вводить — можно просто менять ⬜ на «х» или «+».)
ControlType.Text |
ControlType.Text | Так колонка «Контакт» показывает детально по каналам, а общий «Статус» остаётся для школы в целом (Отправлено / Есть ответ).
ControlType.Text |
ControlType.Text | Если захочешь вместо этого
ControlType.Text | настоящие кликабельные галочки
ControlType.Text |  — это делается через отдельную колонку под каждый канал (в Google Таблицах: выделить ячейки → Вставка → Флажок). Но тогда каналы придётся разнести по отдельным столбцам, и таблица станет шире. Скажи, если такой вариант удобнее — перестрою.

Dear GASB team,
My family has recently relocated to Batumi, and my main goal for this summer is to help my two children (ages 9 and 11) make real, serious progress in English.
I saw your Summer Academic Inquiry Labs (SAIL) summer school, which looks wonderful - but unfortunately I couldn't find full information on your website, so I'd love to learn more directly.
A summer camp would be great, but I don't want to limit myself to it and possibly miss something more suitable. Could you tell me about all the options you offer for children this summer - for example:
- The SAIL summer school (dates, daily schedule, price, age groups);
- Any other English intensives or programmes, including residential options if you have them;
- Small-group or one-to-one lessons, if available.
It would also help to know:
- Are the classes taught by native / US English teachers?
- How do you assess and handle different levels?
- What is the enrolment process?
My priority is a real breakthrough in the language, so I'm open to any format you would recommend for that.
Thank you very much - I look forward to hearing from you.
Best regards,
Ana

Who are we?
The British Center is the exclusive representative of the English Callan Method Organization (CMO) in Georgia, which was founded in 2003 and is currently the largest English language school in the country.
The school began operating in 2003 with minimal resources. Specifically, in a small building with only three auditoriums for students.
The British Center was the first school to introduce the Callan Method in Georgia, thereby revolutionizing the field of English language learning.
Our team is staffed with highly qualified teachers, and the quality of teaching is managed and controlled by the English Callan Method Organization (CMO).
Every year, thousands of individual students study English at the British Center, while our corporate clients include both government agencies and private companies operating in various fields of business.

Enjoy a stay in our newly renovated 2-bedroom apartment with a balcony and sea view, just a few minutes’ walk from the beach and Batumi Boulevard. The apartment is bright, clean, and fully equipped with everything you need — Wi-Fi, TV, full kitchen, and comfortable living space. Its great location means you’re close to cafes, shops, and city attractions, making it easy to explore and relax at the same time.The spaceWe are a small family-run business offering newly renovated 2-bedroom apartments just a short walk from the Batumi seaside. Each apartment has two separate bedrooms with queen-size beds and a sofa in the living room that can be converted into an additional single bed. You’ll enjoy a modern, fully equipped kitchen and a stylish, very clean bathroom. Our apartments are bright, cozy, and designed for your comfort, making them perfect for families, friends, or couples looking to relax and enjoy Batumi.Guest accessWe strive to make check-in as simple and convenient as possible. You’ll receive the exact location on Google Maps to easily find the apartment, as well as an extra PDF guide with helpful tips for your stay.Our building’s main door and elevator are secured with locks, and you’ll be provided with a personal PIN for easy access. The apartment itself is equipped with smart locks — you’ll receive the password plus one set of keys for your convenience.We aim to make your stay smooth, safe, and stress-free from the moment you arrive.Other things to noteWe kindly remind you that the apartment is newly renovated, and we strive to keep it clean and polished for all our guests.The apartment is smoke-free — please do not smoke inside.Please leave everything neat and tidy upon check-out.Guests are responsible for any damages and may need to replace or pay for broken items.Kitchen countertops are made of real stone and can be damaged or stained. Please avoid standing on them and do not place colorful food directly on the surface. Clean immediately after cooking.Please unplug the iron and hair dryer when leaving the apartment.We appreciate your care and understanding in helping us maintain the apartment for everyone’s comfort.

ControlType.Text | Клод, вот что мне ответил British Centre
Hi, we are happy to offer you a Super Minds course for children aged 6-12. It represents the Cambridge University’s latest method of English for kids. The complete course consists of 7 stages. The duration of each stage is approximately 5-6 months. Monthly tuition fee is 350 GEL, which includes the textbooks and audio-video resources. If you choose morning or afternoon hours, you will study for 250 GEL instead of 350 GEL until the end of July; Two 50-minute lessons are held in groups 3 times per week.
We work from Monday to Saturday from 9 am until 9 pm. You can choose your desired schedule yourself. You can choose either Monday-Wednesday-Friday or Tuesday-Thursday-Saturday for your classes.
The maximum number of children in a group is 10.
We have qualified and certified Georgian teachers who are experienced in teaching young learners using the Super Minds programme.
It is possible to enroll for the courses every day. If you wish to register, you can visit us at the Batumi branch, which is located at the corner of 31 Chavchavadze Street and 56 Luka Asatiani Street. alternatively, you can reach us on the phone: 591 00 82 88. We would also like to add that our placement test is free of charge. Furthermore, you can attend 3 trial lessons for free.

ControlType.Text | Dear British Centre team,  I am writing to introduce my family and to ask for your guidance. We are relocating to Batumi for the summer, and my priority is for my two children - aged 9 and 11 - to make serious, sustained progress in their English.  I have read about the British Centre with great interest: as the exclusive representative of the Callan Method Organization in Georgia and the largest English-language school in the country, you have exactly the standing and quality of teaching I am hoping to find for them. It would be a real privilege for my children to study with you.  Unfortunately, I could not find detailed information online about your summer programmes, so I am reaching out directly. I am open to any format the school runs over the summer - a summer camp, an intensive course, or regular lesson-based classes - whatever would best suit children of their age and this goal.  To help me plan, I would be very grateful if you could tell me:  What programmes do you offer for children this summer, and which would you recommend for ages 9 and 11? What are the available dates, the daily or weekly schedule, and the duration of each course? How large are the groups, and would a 9- and an 11-year-old be placed together or separately? Do you assess each child's level beforehand, and how do you handle different levels? Who teaches the children - are the teachers Callan-certified and/or native English speakers? What are the fees, and what is the enrolment process? Thank you very much for your time. I look forward to hearing what you would recommend for them.  With kind regards, Ana  P.S. I'm sending this same message through a few of your other contacts as well, just to make sure it reaches you - so apologies in advance for the small duplication.
Сб 20:40
Hi, we are happy to offer you a Super Minds course for children aged 6-12. It represents the Cambridge University’s latest method of English for kids. The complete course consists of 7 stages. The duration of each stage is approximately 5-6 months. Monthly tuition fee is 350 GEL, which includes the textbooks and audio-video resources. If you choose morning or afternoon hours, you will study for 250 GEL instead of 350 GEL until the end of July; Two 50-minute lessons are held in groups 3 times per week.
We work from Monday to Saturday from 9 am until 9 pm. You can choose your desired schedule yourself. You can choose either Monday-Wednesday-Friday or Tuesday-Thursday-Saturday for your classes.
The maximum number of children in a group is 10.
We have qualified and certified Georgian teachers who are experienced in teaching young learners using the Super Minds programme.
It is possible to enroll for the courses every day. If you wish to register, you can visit us at the Batumi branch, which is located at the corner of 31 Chavchavadze Street and 56 Luka Asatiani Street. alternatively, you can reach us on the phone: 591 00 82 88. We would also like to add that our placement test is free of charge. Furthermore, you can attend 3 trial lessons for free.
